Floral fragrance for women and men. <b>Soleil Blanc</b> was launched in 2016. The nose behind this fragrance is Natalie Gracia-Cetto. Top notes are Pistachio, Bergamot, Cardamom and Pink Pepper; middle notes are Tuberose, Ylang-Ylang and Jasmine; base notes are Coconut, Amber, Tonka Bean and Benzoin. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Tom Ford Soleil Blanc is unexpected, sultry and addictive solar floral scent. It evokes emote private islands where summer lasts all year. Tom Ford’s latest private blend creation unapologetically exudes the endless pursuit of sun and luxury that defines Tom Ford Soleil.</p>

<p>The top note of the unisex fragrance combines spicy notes of cardamom and pink pepper with a hint of pistachio and bergamot. Flowery sensuality of ylang ylang, Egyptian jasmine and tuberose are placed in the heart of the fragrance for carnal intensity. Benzoin a herbal substance contained in oil of bitter almonds, amber, tonka bean and coconut milk form the luxurious base. </p>

<p> 
Available as 50, 100 and 250 ml Eau de Parfum.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2322433" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="sassa7"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/114217"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.114217.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="sassa7" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Korres/Black-Sugar-63257.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.63257.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Black Sugar"title="Black Sugar"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2322433ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2322433" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/114217">sassa7</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-21">10/21/24 01:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think it's the cardamom-coconut to blame for the sun tan lotion vibe, same as in Crystal Noir's tanning lotion signature scent, again cardamom-coconut, even though that's a different very woody pencil shavings scent. Also, petitgrain with lavender for Libre's suntan lotion vibe aaaand cardamom with lavender for a subtle masculine tanning lotion impression in Korres Vetiver Root. BBW Getaway Soiree is more balsamic-churchy kinda like MK Wonderlust Sublime. If you don't wanna spend the money, go for DUA's Where Sun Never Sets. For balsamic tropical scents like tanning lotion without the coconut, I prefer Very Sexy Oasis and MK Wonderlust Sublime. <br />
<br />
This family of solar tanning lotion perfumes utilize indolic white florals to amplify the tanning lotion effect or to even create such impression from scratch when they are coconut-free so more sophisticated to me; the tanning lotion vibe is just more intense and playful in scents like this one with the coconut- cardamom. So they play around with indolic beachy notes like Tiare flower as in MK Wonderlust Sublime, or with Tuberose as we have it here, in Getaway Soiree and in Very Sexy Oasis, alone or paired with solar florals like the solar -sometimes camphor-like - waxy and salty orange blossom, as in Very Sexy Oasis and MK Wonderlust Sublime, drenched in balsamic syrupy amber for that 'liquid gold' feel that Wonderlust Sublime has. Another solar note they use in conjunction with indolic white flowers is the ylang ylang for a similar to orange blossom solar vibe, only less salty-waxy, that we have here and in Tropidelic - where it mimics the camphor-like stinky side of orange blossom - in Tropidelic I mean. These are all fueled by amber, as all of the above or vanilla as in BBW Sunkissed, another tanning lotion solar scent without the coconut, but with salty vanilla instead for a beachy feel, again orange blossom-infused. The benzoin here also adds warmth and balsam along with the amber. Libre YSL reinforces its more fresh tanning lotion impression with its solar orange blossom and mandarin. Getaway Soiree has mandarin too, so you see these solar beachy perfumes have some lovely common points. I usually gravitate towards tuberose-heavy scents like this one and Getaway Soiree/Very Sexy Oasis, even tho they are more syrupy and heady balsamic. Some other solar scents in this genre that I like include Borabora Giardini Di Toscana/DUA Hug Of Flowers and Oud Jaune Intense Fragrance du Bois/ DUA Aoud Intense Sunlight <br />
<br />
In this solar ambery-syrupy league, but less beachy and more in the sense of sunny valleys and dusty yellow flowers are scents like the heady BBW Golden Sunflower with its orange blossom and dusty sunflower, and Gingham Glow or 'Gingham Gold' as I tend to call it, with its playful and youthfully sweet 'golden nectar', the syrupy, slightly dusty marigold note and the 'sun soaked ambery sandalwood'. There are a ton more out there in this happy 'chasing the sun' family.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="2322433"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=2322433#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77); It is a mystery to me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="2320099"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=2320099#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2319919" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The notes describe it perfectly. It’s a slightly tropical (not in the overly sweet, fruity or cloying sense but in the fresh, beachy and warm sense) coconut and light white floral scent. The coconut note in it is not sweet at all, think more “i just scaled that coconut tree and cracked one open” type of smell. I do get a very faint sun cream/ sun lotion type of scent from it too which I personally really like, as well as a warm solar note from it. A perfect summer scent :)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="2215351"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=2215351#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2213730" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1174716">spyral.1</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-17">05/17/24 10:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Of all the beachy scents on the market (and I have tried them all), nothing really transports me to a summer getaway like Soleil Blanc. I did not want to love this because of the price tag, but this fragrance is smooth and balmy and warms beautifully on the skin in the heat. The coconut never gets too sweet, the white florals are elegant, and the spices add texture without being overbearing. It's a beautifully blended masterpiece. I wish it projected a bit more, and lasted a bit longer, so I will never purchase this at full price. However, it will always be one I reach for when I need a mood boost on a scorching summer day.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="2159140"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=2159140#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2143170" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1478553">suzanne_ronald</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-26">04/26/24 05:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A Private Tom Ford Beach Party...<br />
<br />
This smells like a scent that Tom Ford would make, although I wasn't sure what to expect before I tried it, given Tom's penchant for square &amp; black silhouettes.   Would it be a sharper image white, like the artist's whiter whites and blacker blacks?  But no...this heads in a different - but equally Tom Ford - direction: it's more of a sexy white...<br />
<br />
I just have a sample of this, but I've tested it a few times now.  Evokes a beach party full of glamorous people in couture swimwear, sun-bronzed and growing musky under a white-hot sun.  Overall it's a really well blended scent, although all the individual notes are there. There's a nice cooling tropical vibe in the top notes, with a fluffy, powdery white-floral beachiness in the heart.  In the base, I do get the coconut &amp; animalics - the notes previously listed civet, but that's been removed for some reason - although the civettone here is really well blended into the base.  Performance is excellent for a summer scent profile, and good enough for wearing throughout the year.  For uniqueness it's a love for me.  8/10.  Enjoy!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="2136870"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=2136870#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2120230" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Update for longevity: I’m pleasantly surprised that a “light” scent profile of this kind lasted fairly well. I sprayed around 3 pm and I still get whiffs of it once close up to my arm. I forgot I even had it on until I was watching a clip on my phone and thought what’s that beautiful smell. It’s the perfume! One spray on my arm without lotion or oil lasted 9 hours. Of course to be noticed by the scent in a room is only in the first 2-4 hours.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="2098560"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=2098560#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2098412" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; One of them was very coconutty and I couldn’t remember which one. I bought SB a week ago and the scent is very very overpowering to me. I mean two sprays on my neck and I feel nauseous from the amount of white flowers. <br />
Edit: it had to grow on me and now I can’t stop wearing it. I got this perfume because I wanted something more feminine for spring/summer. This smells very clique and solar. When I wear this I feel very classy and clean. The white flowers had to grow on me since it had been a while but now I’m in love! I have a love-hate relationship with white florals. A tuberose fragrance that has a certain creaminess from a note like coconut = love. A tuberose with a bunch of heady white florals = hate. Which is why I could bathe in fragrances like this or carnal flower. The tuberose here is dominant and very present, but not like the one you smell in stuff like My Way or L’interdit, which are quite suffocating and headache-inducing to me personally. The pistachio and the coconut keep this smooth and creamy (as in “texture”, not lactonic creamy) throughout, and the ylang ylang keeps it tropical and sunny. <br />
Shame about the performance though. I get through a full bottle before summer is over.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="2086455"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=2086455#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2080708" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Exotic. Unexpected. Refined. Sensual. Creamy and persuasive fragrance that evokes remote tropical atmospheres, wonderful uncontaminated islands of the Pacific where summer lasts all year round and uncontaminated and lush nature pervades the senses with its heavenly scents. Soleil Blanc by Tom Ford is an intoxicating symphony of largely citrus notes fused with solar amber redundant with refined floral notes of: Ylang Ylang, tuberose and orange blossom and enlivened by green notes of Galbanum and seductive creamy notes of coconut, which crave with impunity the infinite search for the sun. A fragrance that evolves in a reassuring way until it vanishes completely...unfortunately on my skin it vanishes like a wonderful dream upon waking.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1904503">celiasdream</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-28">12/28/23 20:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Captures the affluent-Americana of a TF film. A housewife on an escapist vacation, chopping her hair off and dying it in the sink; a beat-down luxury car driving through the desert at night. The sum of the sunny notes is greater than any individual part, transcending from frivolous to mysterious. The storytelling that lacks in a movie like Nocturnal Animals is perfected here, with all the stunning visuals summoned by mixing hearty amber into upscale florals. I have just a few drops of this left in the bottle I got in July 2022, kicking off my interest in fragrance, but I save it for whenever I want to feel like a crisp, sheer white button-down, unironed, billowing across luminescently over-spray-tanned skin in a 2000s fashion mag.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1784272">kittenpawz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-27">12/27/23 21:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Alien Goddess is my signature and I finally got to test Soleil Blanc. Totally the same scent profile as Alien Goddess and also love at first sniff for me. Comparing the two I would also say that it's more modern-smelling, much less powdery than AG (I'd even say it is instead a tad juicy/sparkly) and performance is about the same. I'd thought it was a very strong perfume since I could smell it through my clothes even when I had a coat on but it disappeared faster than other perfumes I had on that I considered weak. It's less citrusy which I personally love but regrettably doesn't evolve much (and I thought the same of the other Tom Ford fragrance I sampled). My sweater still smells of it and it's the same scent I smelled when I first sprayed it and the same scent I last smelled before it was gone. But lots of people are fine with linear fragrances as long as they smell good and Soleil Blanc is amazing scent-wise and has a high quality DNA. <br />
<br />
I'm not a fan of either cardamom or pepper or bergamot but they are not overbearing in this fragrance and didn't bother me at all. Soleil Blanc is not necessarily reminiscent of sunscreen but does smell like vacation and has a truly opulent quality to it. It's joyous, refined and youthful. Although best suited for hot summer days, I wouldn't savor it for such days only, for it is so good it should be enjoyed every chance you get.<br />
<br />
If you love Alien Goddess, you will love this also. In general if you're fond of sweet and feminine tropical/beachy/mediterranean-like coconut scents with hints of spice/sourness, you can't go wrong with Soleil Blanc.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Creamy, coconutty tuberose scent. Smells like sunscreen a bit but not in an offensive way. It definitely dries down to be a lot more nutty from the pistachio. <br />
<br />

I do also use the shimmering body oil (not together, but I should try it!) because the price is much lower, and I find that the fragrance is exactly the same, and the performance is fairly close too! The perfume does have a little better longevity and projection, but I’m impressed that with the shimmering body oil that I can still smell it on myself the next morning and people don’t have to be right up against me to smell it (I always get a lot of compliments!)! I don’t normally like tuberose (can smell too much like bubble gum or tablet candy) or ylang ylang (can smell too much like banana) but I don’t get those leanings in this. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1977762" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JosephFragrance"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1689650"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1689650.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JosephFragrance" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1977762ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1977762" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1689650">JosephFragrance</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-16">11/16/23 02:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tom Ford Soleil Blanc: A Sweet Symphony of Sunlit Opulence<br />
<br />
Tom Ford Soleil Blanc, a radiant gem in the Private Blend collection, beckons you to embark on a journey to sun-drenched shores and tropical bliss. From the first tantalizing spritz, Soleil Blanc unveils a world of opulence that is uniquely sweet, making it a standout among the masterpieces of Tom Ford.<br />
<br />
The opening notes transport you to a luxurious oasis, where bergamot and cardamom intermingle with a touch of pink pepper, setting the stage for the intoxicating blend that unfolds. What distinguishes Soleil Blanc is its artful infusion of sweetness—subtle, refined, and utterly captivating. The creamy pistachio note adds a delightful nuance, creating a velvety texture that feels like a caress of the warm sun on your skin.<br />
<br />
As the fragrance evolves, the floral heart notes, including ylang-ylang and tuberose, blossom with tropical allure, evoking the essence of exotic blooms in full bloom. The sweet interplay of coconut and jasmine adds depth, transforming Soleil Blanc into a harmonious symphony that lingers delicately in the air.<br />
<br />
What makes Soleil Blanc truly remarkable, in my opinion, is its unique position as the sweet jewel within the Tom Ford lineup. While Tom Ford is often synonymous with sophisticated and bold fragrances, Soleil Blanc stands out as a testament to the brand's versatility. It's a fragrance that effortlessly transitions from day to night, from casual elegance to formal allure, making it a delightful companion for a myriad of occasions.<br />
<br />
The longevity of Soleil Blanc is commendable, ensuring that its sunlit sweetness accompanies you throughout the day. The bottle, a vision of pristine white and gold, encapsulates the essence of luxury that Tom Ford is renowned for.<br />
<br />
In conclusion, Tom Ford Soleil Blanc is more than a fragrance; it's an escape to a sun-soaked paradise where sweetness meets sophistication. Its ability to seamlessly blend opulence with sweetness makes it a rare gem in the Tom Ford collection. As you indulge in its exquisite allure, you'll find yourself transported to a world of indulgence, warmth, and enduring beauty.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662712">WhiteFlowerPrincess</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-01">11/01/23 04:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is absolutely LOVELY! It makes me think of being at a beach of a hotel in a tropical paradise, like Hawaii for example. It has very summery and day time vibes and it smells very feminine and yummy to me.<br />
<br />
I can smell the green and nutty pistachio, the citrusy bergamot and the sweet and spicy cardamom in the opening, but it is only subtle and it doesn't overpower the heart notes at all for me. I can't smell the pink pepper too, which makes me happy, since it isn't my most favorite note ever.<br />
<br />
The creamy and slightly spicy tuberose, banana-sweet ylang-ylang and mildly indolic jasmine then come into play and makes me think of a lush tropical flower bouquet in the lobby of a Hilton or a Sheraton. I mean that in the best possible way though... it's very luxurious smelling!<br />
<br />
In the base notes I can mainly smell a creamy and tropical smelling coconut, but a subtle hint of amber, tonka bean and benzoin are discernible here and there. I think of this fragrance as an equal blend of coconut and white florals, with some spice added here and there. It's kind of like the day time version of Crystal Noir by Versace to me 🥰<br />
<br />
I got 6 hours wear from this perfume and a moderate sillage that was quite lovely. I think that it would only suit day time occasions in the summer because of its casual vibe and its summery notes. I feel like one's skin would intensify the notes most during the summer too.<br />
<br />
Altogether, I'd give Soleil Blanc by Tom Ford an 8.3/10. I definitely reccomed this perfume!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1965733"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1965733#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1962997" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1815219">astrorocks</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-31">08/31/23 13:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is pretty nice. One thing I will always appreciate about Tom Ford is he somehow manages to balance fragrances well enough that, even if I don't LOVE a fragrance or note, it does not bother my nose (which is, admittedly, pretty sensitive). This smells pretty exactly as advertised - expensive suntan lotion at a resort. Something all-expense paid, adults-only in the Caribbean. Not my kind of vacation and, also, not my kind of scent. But it does do precisely what it says and evokes exactly the imagery it claims so, again, if you like that I'd really check this one out. My issue with it is that it is kind of artificial and not very sophisticated (but, then, I'd say that about a lot of fragrances in this category). I can only really see this being worn by a woman in a a very sunny place and time. It dries down way too sugary-sweet and fruity for me after about an hour to enjoy all day - I was expecting it to have more 'bite' with the pepper and amber notes listed but tonka bean and coconut reign supreme here. I agree with other reviewers it is probably overpriced for what it is. Sillage and longevity are not as high as other TF fragrances. But, really, this was never going to be my wheelhouse so another one to not take me too seriously on. It's like a 6.5/10...if I liked these kind of scents I'd probably like this one (but maybe not at this price point).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1916375"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1916375#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1914148" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I thought it was pleasant, pretty. A beachy sunscreen-y sort of vibe.  But then my nose developed a bit more, I could pick out synthetic coconut scents in other fragrances, other beach type scents just didn’t appeal, I was subconsciously using this as the gold standard.  A few years back I purchased a bottle.  Its beautiful in the heat, the only fragrance that gets me compliments, it’s easy to wear and appropriate always.  It layers with Neroli Portofino, Jasmin Rouge, Santal Blush, and other Private Blends to create new fragrant potions. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1888263" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="81ghazal1314"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1730853"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="81ghazal1314" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1888263ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1888263" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1730853">81ghazal1314</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-27">07/27/23 11:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Earlier I made a comment saying this smells like Supreme Bouquet by Yves Saint Laurent. But I've changed my mind after wearing it. The opening is very green on me and stays that way for a couple of minutes. At some point the greenness mixes with the nutty pistachio and  creamy sweetness which made it almost disgusting on me. I don't like nutty scents most of the time in perfumes and it wasn't the good type of greenness. But then after a good couple of minutes it becomes more tolerable. The tuberose is the heart but it's neither realistic nor similar to any tuberose I've smelled before. The pistachio makes it very different. Upclose I don't like it, it has something that reminds me of a fluffy cake that was left outside and has became a little sour and spoiled. But it smells good in the air. And yeh it's definitely feminine, sillage super good, long lasting. Idk it's just not my favorite perfume ever. I expect to be blown away with luxury and beauty for such price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1888263"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1888263#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1888081" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; To me, the coconut scent is so faint that it's barely perceptible. It leans towards a green coconut rather than a creamy one, easily overshadowed by the floral elements. The green tuberose doesn't contribute much either, I would've preferred the sweet kind for this particular blend.<br />
<br />
For me, above all, this perfume is a pure white floral. It's fresh and perfect for hot weather. I do enjoy it, although I had anticipated a more pronounced coconut aroma.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1846983"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1846983#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1843284" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Maybe it’s because I live in Hawaii, so the idea of something with a tropical smell is nice, but I’ve also found it to be a clean and fresh scent for biz travel to the mainland. This lands on my skin as a light and fresh scent, and I like it in biz settings because it doesn’t create a “what are you wearing” reaction (which I have gotten from the more coconut/tropical scent of Soleil de Feu). I’ve been wearing Beachwalk for a few years, then recently picked up Terracotta &amp; Aerin Hibiscus Palm. Avoided this one after smelling and sampling in store a few times. It Kept coming off too citrus at the start, in a way I didn’t like. So I never sprayed on my skin because it didn’t seem like it would be for me.  <br />

The cardamom takes this beach scene to the Middle East for me. And I love it! <br />
Creed VIW is beachside cool drinks in Jaimaica or Mexico. <br />
Beachwalk is muscle beach California. <br />
Terracotta is Sanibel island Florida . <br />
Hibiscus Palm is fresh drinks in Key West all the way. <br />
<br />
Soleil Blanc is beach resort on the Red Sea.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1835298"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1835298#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1835022" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It conveys a message of money and class (while it lasts), not sexiness.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1827425"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1827425#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1826854" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1826854" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="auriks03"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1740409"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="auriks03" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1826854ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1826854" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1740409">auriks03</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-07">05/07/23 03:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If you’re a gourmand person this may not be for you. I mostly got this because everyone mentioned the coconut note and I love a good coconut scent but the coconut in this is very much buried in the floral notes<br />
<br />
When you first spray it I mostly get bergamot and then I’m gonna guess it goes to tuberose because it’s a floral scent I’m not familiar with. The floral I smell is more sharp, kind of powdery and reminiscent of hairspray. <br />
Keeping in mind I don’t even like floral or powdery notes whatsoever so this had already lost me with that. <br />
<br />
I would have liked more Jasmine as it’s more creamy and not so much of a stringent floral. <br />
<br />
Then it kind of fades into cedar wood+floral <br />
<br />
It’s not my cup of tea. I constantly hear people label it as a perfect summer scent but it doesn’t give me that summer beach vibes per se but it smells like something an old rich lady would wear on a yacht. The florals give very much old lady but maybe it’s the white florals that give it a more elevated scent, it kind of reminds you of summer flowers type of vibe where the floral note is just cleaner with a powdery tone. <br />
<br />
Overall I think this fragrance is much more mature than I expected. It’s not an obnoxious old-lady scent but I do think it’s a bit pungent for the summer, maybe more for early to mid spring</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1826854"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1826854#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1825709" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
This really does smell like sun screen. There is coconut but, to me it’s more floral and creamy. Silage is big. My wife always says from across the room “did you put the sunscreen smell on”? Haha. She does not like this one and asks why I would want to smell like sunscreen. <br />
<br />
However, as much as this smells like sunscreen it is too powerful to me to be a summer fragrance. It is heavy and nearly cloying. I also own the Eau De Soleil blanc which to me is much better. It is more versatile, more summery, and less like pure sunscreen smell. <br />
<br />
I do still like this fragrance but it’s more of a token fragrance to me. I wear it to appreciate the pistachio, and coconut creamy goodness. But that’s about it.<br />
<br />
I’ve never gotten a single compliment from it. Actually they ask why I smell like sunscreen. However, I live in a place where it is only sunny 2 months out of the year.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1825709"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1825709#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1822284" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1582152">dabeyondobsessedemperor</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-11">04/11/23 22:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Like most fragrances from Tom Ford's Private Blend line, Soleil Blanc has a specific, and fairly narrow, target audience, but it delivers really well to that audience.<br />
<br />
Soleil Blanc is something I'd wear almost exclusively to the beach: sweet, creamy coconut dominating lighter citruses and florals. It's fairly linear, and entirely tropical, and doesn't really develop over time. Like literally everyone else says, it smells like ultra-bougie sunscreen, like the type you'd expect to find at a private 5-star beach resort. Again, I wouldn't quite wear this anywhere other than the beach.<br />
<br />
I will say that the Soleil Blanc body oil is an excellent moisturizer as well as a fantastic layering piece--several sprays of marine-vibe fragrances, such as Sedley, Mandarino di Amalfi, or even Invictus Aqua, over a modest lather of Soleil Blanc body oil, creates an insanely beautiful, sweet-salty oceanic and tropical accord that perfectly complements your beach, yacht or water sport days.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;                             <div id="parent824466" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc824466" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RubyBirdy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/954069"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="RubyBirdy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Jo-Loves/White-Rose-Lemon-Leaves-37576.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.37576.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="White Rose & Lemon Leaves"title="White Rose & Lemon Leaves"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma824466ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd824466" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/954069">RubyBirdy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-20">05/20/17 14:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is one of the perfumes which I file away in the category of, "Nice, But Not for That Price." Soleil Blanc is a fun, pleasant sunscreen-style fragrance, a creamy coconut-floral with good longevity that just screams summertime. It's straightforward and not the most cerebral fragrance, but sometimes that's nice. For $60, I would buy this. For $200+? Oh, no no no. Too simple to demand that amount of money. You have to be joking.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="824466"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=824466#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1347596" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1347596" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="malescent"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1266473"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1266473.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="malescent" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1347596ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1347596" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1266473">malescent</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-05-22">05/22/21 09:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I went out on a mission to find a “refined coconut summer fragrance” for my woman, at her request, since she “trusts my nose”..so after a filter search here on fragrantica, I visited my familiar Tom Ford sales assistant in order to sample both soleil blancs as I already suppose, based on olfactory memory and her preferences on fragrances, that the usual suspect virgin island water is not something she would opt for..so this comparing review is based on single wear on me and take that into account before you decide for yourselves. Also take into account that the testing was done on a 26 degrees Celsius day..<br />
<br />
Eau de soleil blanc starts with citrus before transitioning to a coconut creamy white floral fragrance.<br />
Soleil blanc on the other hand lacks this citrus, has a beautiful modest almond feeling(maybe the pistachio listed here?)<br />
Projection was better on eau de soleil without that meaning that it was not decent from the soleil blanc. I got constant whafs from both my arms throughout the day. <br />
I cannot comment on silage of both as it was a single spot spray—single wear but the one I eventually bought for my woman has great silage!<br />
Longevity at least 8 hours (on the 8 hour mark I showered) with the soleil blanc persisting on my skin even after showering for what it’s worth.<br />
<br />
Note here that despite the “eau” in the name of the bottle of one, they are both edp concentrations.<br />
<br />
I understand that to the average nose out there, and let’s face it, this is the vast majority of your encounters, this fragrance will give the impression of suntan lotion. But to be honest it is not. It is a luxury feeling coconut note, creamy, milky if I may say, almost gourmand, relaxing, dancing beautifully with pistachio especially in the soleil blanc bottle. <br />
<br />
Main differences between the two?<br />
<br />
The “sand” feeling (I do not know which note in the perfume emits this vibe but it is certainly there) is to me present in the eau de soleil blanc only and it is absent from the soleil blanc variant. It gives you the impression that you get the smell of thin light brown sand, warmed after being exposed to the sun, on your skin. <br />
<br />
Another difference is the fact that the citruses are more present throughout the lifespan of the eau de soleil blanc, prominent in the opening and taking a backstage in the drydown.This citrus presence is not easily detectable in the drydown of soleil blanc, which in turn is to me a better blend in total.<br />
<br />
Masculine or feminine?<br />
<br />
And in order to address the elephant in the room, are they both more masculine or feminine? Before I write down my opinion, it is interesting to tell you this: when I went to the sales assistant, who knows my preferences rather well by now, from a lot of previous encounters, and asked to sample those fragrances, her first response was “I do not believe this is something you would wear..those two scents might be rather feminine leaning for your taste”. Now before you judge her comment, I personally understand where it comes from, taking into account her preconceived notion about me based on my past purchases and I love that about her because this is truly a personalized and customized service from an employee who loves her job. She also went on to explain that the customer demographic of those two as far as sales go, is mostly women. To be clear fragrances have no genders and I do not judge people by what they like to smell. Based on note breakdown one would guess that maybe the presence of citruses in eau de soleil blanc is something that could make this more “easy” for a man to wear it and that is understandable. Maybe the eau de soleil is the fragrance of the two that men would prefer because of those citruses alone, creating a more airy feeling. <br />
<br />
For me, the only scenario I would wear any of them would be while on the beach, while on vacation and the one I would opt for believe it or not is the soleil blanc. It is more elegant than its sibling to my nose and if you decide to go down the road of coconut then rock it all the way. I truly believe that this fragrance, on a self assured man, relaxing on the beach, would be spot on and somewhat different from all the usual citrus smelling scents out there. And if you are in your 30s (I am older!) it may attract for you some new encounters because women like this scent! Now smelling this on a man in a dinner restaurant scenario for example, may feel at least to me somewhat out of place. Instead smelling this on a woman, especially in summer, regardless of the scenario makes me think that she is a woman of taste and elegance.<br />
<br />
Final thoughts:<br />
<br />
My woman fell in love with it when I bought it for her..She wore it a lot in summer..I loved smelling it on her..I think she smells elegant,sexy,alluring wearing this scent..Her, in a summer dress, warm breeze giving me whafs of this from her, makes me literally craving to go d@wn on her..this scent on her, this creamy almond feeling pistachio, white floral, coconut combination is truly an invisible magnet..<br />
<br />
Is it versatile? For a woman yes, for a man maybe not so much. The only scenario I could rock this is while on the beach and I may even enjoy it like Virgin Island Water, the fragrance I usually opt for when I am on summer vacation.<br />
<br />
But by now the smell of soleil blanc to my mind is already an olfactory representation of her, elegantly dressed in white, in the summer night, smiling at me with her black piercing eyes..<br />
<br />
Is it year round? No..except if one wants to take an olfactory trip while at home, during a winter day, anticipating summer holidays perhaps?<br />
<br />
Is it signature worthy?No..even for a woman I cannot picture this as a signature everyday scent..I truly don’t know why..<br />
<br />
Is it worth the price asked? Eventually it is not a versatile all year round fragrance and under this scope for some it may not worth the price. But for the scenarios that this fragrance fits, the quality of this scent for me justifies the price.<br />
<br />
Trust only your nose..it was a single wear for me, but I experienced it enough on my significant half throughout last summer..<br />
<br />
Smell nice and smile!!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="1347596"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=1347596#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1069274" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/494286">Kon-nos91</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-06-11">06/11/19 14:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>How does this smell like? Like summer in Greece. Don't judge it immediately after spraying it, let it dry for at least 30' and then...it smells like a feeling.<br />
<br />
No, I don't have anything to win from TF, mostly from Private Collection that is so expensive (70% not worthy) but, this perfume is a success story. You wake up in a Greek island, morning sea breeze awakens your soul, bright sun gives you the need to go to the beach. You apply cream suntan lotion, no matter how 'glamorous' or not. After your sunbathing, your skin is sunkissed and treated with sea's salt. This is exactly what Soleil Blanc reminds me of. This thing must be experienced to get my point. The only notes that can clearly detect are: Cardamom, TF's tuberose, a touch of amber &amp; benzoin and a whisper of real coconut/pistachio leaves.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/884106">ShiveringTimber</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-05-07">05/07/18 20:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I live an oxymoron. I've only been on a beach ... one time, in nearly 40 years of life. I prefer my urban dwelling that is surrounded by the Smoky Mountains. But, give me a tropical, coconut cologne and I suddenly become a beach bum on my balcony overlooking non-stop traffic. Maybe that's one of the best parts about fragrances? I'm stuck where I'm at for awhile and these beachy scents let me get away ... sort of. Most of the problems others have noted with this Tom Ford are not happening to me. I have a very nice, somewhat sweet coconut with some light florals floating around behind it. I don't know if I would buy a full bottle but I find scents like these are worth buying a 1.7 of or if you have a trusted decanter to sell you a 20-30 ml decant of. I'm kind of stuck on whether I like this or Creed's Virgin Island Water better. I do think the VIW is more masculine than the Soleil Blanc but both are now in my spring/summer rotation. Check back in September, I'll be all out of these two and the heat of the summer will have me begging for cold weather and I'll be swearing off coconuts for good. It's a cycle, you should try it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="34893"comment_id="940500"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-Blanc-34893.html?ccid=940500#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent946060" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

<br />
